# Fine Tuning Jobs Operations \{#fine-tuning/jobs\}

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs\}

_Get Fine Tuning Jobs_

Get a list of fine-tuning jobs for your organization and user.

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="default">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job\}

Create a new fine-tuning job, it will be queued for processing.

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\}/cancel \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job\}

_Cancel Fine Tuning Job_

Request the cancellation of a fine tuning job.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

### Parameters \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs+operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job+operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_job+operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job+parameters\}

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content" variant="top-level">

##### job\_id <Pill variant="warning">required</Pill> \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs+operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job+operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_job+operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job+parameters+job_id\}

The ID of the job to cancel.

</SectionContent>

</Section>
